9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The company is a wholly owned subsidiary of Canary Wharf Group plc and its ultimate parent<a /> undertaking is Songbird Estates plc.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span><ix:nonNumeric name="ns1:DescriptionPrincipalActivities" contextRef="CY_PERIOD">The principal activity of the company is  building contracting.</ix:nonNumeric></span> All activities take place<a /> within the United Kingdom. The directors are not aware, at the date of this report,<a /> of any likely major changes in the company's activities in the coming year.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Construction is continuing on the Riverside South site which was pre-sold to JP Morgan in<a /> 2008. JP Morgan has the option of not proceeding with further construction on this site<a /> following completion of works up to street level.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>If construction of the Riverside South<a /> building does not continue, the company will be paid for the completed work and also retain<a /> £76.0 million representing a portion of the developer's profits relating to the development (of which £68.5 million had been received by the year end).<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>If JP Morgan proceeds with full construction, additional fees will be due.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: 2009.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The station<a /> will include around 100,000 sq ft of additional retail space.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Work on the station box is<a /> on budget and on schedule for completion in 2012.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span in the company's profit and loss account, the company's profit after tax for the<a /> year was £836,715 (2009: £3,277,721). </span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: indicates that<a /> net assets were £1,051,293 (2009: £3,514,578). Details of amounts owed to group companies are shown in Note 11.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a Canary Wharf Group (comprising Canary Wharf Group plc and its subsidiaries)<a /> manages its operations on a unified basis.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>For this reason, the company's<a /> directors believe that key performance indicators specific to the company are not<a /> necessary or appropriate for an understanding of the development, performance or<a /> position of its business.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The performance of the Canary Wharf Group, which<a /> includes the company, is discussed in the Annual Report of Canary Wharf Group plc,<a /> which does not form part of this report.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">PRINCIPAL RISKS <span>AND</span> UNCERTAINTIES</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">As a member of the Canary Wharf Group the key risks facing the company include the cyclical nature of the property and construction markets, financing risk and concentration risk.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Cyclical Nature of the Property and Construction Markets</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The core construction business of the company is subject to many external economic and<a /> market factors which are cyclical in nature.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The turmoil in the financial markets during<a /> 2008 and 2009 was reflected in the property and construction markets by such factors as the<a /> oversupply of available space in the office market, a significant decline in tenant demand<a /> for space in London and a change in the market perception of property as an investment<a /> resulting in a negative impact on property valuations in general and a reduction in<a /> construction activity.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>In the latter half of 2009 and during the course of 2010 there have<a /> been signs of a tightening of supply which has resulted in an increase in valuations and a<a /> compression of yields. Changes in financial and property markets are kept under constant<a /> review so that the company can react appropriately.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The impact of the ongoing uncertainty in the property, construction and financial markets continues to be closely monitored.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Financing Risk</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The broader economic cycle inevitably leads to movements in inflation, interest rates and<a /> bond yields. The company finances its operations largely through surplus cash and<a /> intercompany finance. The ongoing financial markets' uncertainty continues to significantly<a /> limit the availability of funding. In common with other UK property companies, such lack of<a /> financing facilities may have an impact on the business of Canary Wharf Group if the lending markets remain limited for the foreseeable future.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Concentration Risk</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The majority of Canary Wharf Group's real estate assets, including the assets of the<a /> company, are currently located on or adjacent to the Canary Wharf Estate, with tenants that<a /> are mainly linked to the financial services industry.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Wherever possible steps are taken to mitigate or avoid material consequences arising from this concentration.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The principal risks facing the Canary Wharf Group are discussed in the Annual Report of<a /> Canary Wharf Group plc, which does not form part of this report.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">POLICIES</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Payment of creditors</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">In respect of the company's suppliers it is the company's policy to settle the terms of<a /> payment with those suppliers when agreeing the terms of each transaction, ensure that those suppliers are made aware of the terms of payment and abide by the terms of payment.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The number of days of purchases outstanding at 31 December 2010 was 2 (2009: 2).</span></p></div><div><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB; mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br /></span></div><div class="Section6"><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Employment</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The company has adopted the terms of the Code of Practice for the elimination of<a /> discrimination, on all grounds, including disability discrimination.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>To effect this policy<a /> the company has implemented a continuing programme of action with the aim of providing an<a /> equal working environment where all employees are treated with respect and dignity.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The<a /> company continues to keep employees informed of events relevant to their employment via<a /> 'all staff' communications and an intranet. Staff consultative committees, at which matters<a /> raised by employees are considered by management and staff representatives, have been established and meet every two months. The company's employment policy is regularly reviewed to incorporate changes to legislation and ensure best practice is maintained.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Equal opportunities</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The company is committed to equality of opportunity and it is the policy of the company to<a /> make all employment decisions based on the applicant's ability, experience and<a /> qualification without regard to age, sex, race, colour, sexual orientation, ethnic origin, disability or marital status. The company values the benefits a diverse workforce can bring.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The company embraces diversity as a practical contribution to its business success.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Due consideration is given to the recruitment, promotion, training and working conditions of<a /> all employees including those with disabilities. In the event of an employee becoming disabled the company uses its best endeavours to ensure continuity of employment.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Training and development</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The policy of the company is to continuously develop its workforce with the aim of<a /> maximising its success in the marketplace. The training and development of staff is,<a /> therefore, integral to the business process. An annual appraisal programme enables the assessment of individual performance, progress and career prospects within the company.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Health and Safety</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">It is the Canary Wharf Group's policy, within which the company operates, that the working<a /> conditions of its employees incorporate the best standards of health, safety and welfare<a /> that can reasonably be achieved and that all group premises are maintained as safe<a /> environments. Accordingly, adequate resources are made available for these purposes and procedures exist to enable all staff to be informed and consulted on health and safety matters and to make known their views.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">When striving to create the best standards of the built environment the Canary Wharf Group<a /> seeks to promote a safe and healthy environment for its employees, tenants and visitors.<a /> The Canary Wharf Group's continuing commitment to ensuring such a safe and healthy environment is embodied into the formally adopted group health, safety and welfare policy. All legislation relating to health and safety is observed both in letter and in spirit.</span></p></div><div><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB; mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br /></span></div><div class="Section7"><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Environmental</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The company is committed to fully understanding the environmental and social impact of<a /> development on the Estate and of outside projects as appropriate.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>As a result, it is also<a /> committed to applying environmental best practice wherever practical in the design,<a /> construction and management of buildings and their surroundings for the benefit of tenants,<a /> employees, the local community, shareholders and the environment. As a member of the Canary<a /> Wharf Group, the company has maintained <span>ISO</span> 14001 accreditation since early 2005 with environmental management being an inherent part of construction since 2002.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The company is<a /> a member of the Considerate Constructors Scheme and the Better Building Partnership and via Canary Wharf Group plc, the UK Green Building Council and the Green500.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Environmental responsibility</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The Canary Wharf Group plc board retains overall responsibility for the monitoring and<a /> implementation of the group's environmental policy and is assisted by the group's<a /> Environmental Management Review Group which comprises senior executives of the group. A<a /> clear governance process has been developed and implemented to enable the Environmental Management Review Group, and ultimately the board, to identify, manage and respond to the environmental and social risks and opportunities that may affect the group's operations.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The Environmental Management Review Group is responsible for the development and<a /> establishment of the Environmental Management System throughout the group which has been<a /> developed to focus attention on those objectives and targets where improvements and actions<a /> are necessary to meet the monitoring and reporting process formally adopted by the group.<a /> Identified Environmental System Managers have responsibility for the implementation of the<a /> Environmental Management System throughout their respective business areas.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Employee environmental awareness is key to the success of the Environmental Management System and as a result is incorporated into the staff induction programme with regular updates via in-house newsletters and presentations.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The group publishes annually a separate Corporate Social Responsibility Report which<a /> provides details of performance against specified targets and objectives. This report<a /> together with additional supporting information and group publications, can be downloaded<a /> from the group's website.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The group environmental policies are also set out in full on<a /> this website.</span></p></div><div><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB; mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br /></span></div><div class="Section8"><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">STATEMENT AS TO DISCLOSURE OF INFORMATION TO AUDITORS</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><div><ix:nonNumeric name="ns2:StatementOnQualityCompletenessInformationProvidedToAuditors" contextRef="CY_PERIOD"><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Each director holding office at the date of  this report has taken all the steps that he<a /> ought to have  taken as a director in order to make himself aware of relevant audit<a /> information and to establish that the company's auditors are  aware of that information.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>As<a /> far as the directors are aware, there is no relevant audit  information of which the<a /> company's auditors are unaware.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><a /><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">This confirmation is given and should be  interpreted in accordance with the provisions of<a /> Section  418(2) of the Companies Act mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br /></span></div><div class="Section9"><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><div><ix:nonNumeric name="ns2:DirectorsAcknowledgeTheirResponsibilitiesUnderCompaniesAct" contextRef="CY_PERIOD"><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><a /><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;  color:black">The directors are responsible for preparing the report and the  financial statements in<a /> accordance with applicable law and  regulations.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><a /><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Company law requires the directors to prepare  financial statements for each financial year.<a /> Under that  law the directors have elected to prepare the financial statements in  accordance<a /> with United Kingdom Generally Accepted  Accounting Practice (United Kingdom Accounting<a /> Standards  and applicable law). Under company law the directors must not approve the<a /> financial statements unless they are satisfied that they give  a true and fair view of the state of affairs of the company and of the profit  or loss of the company for that period.<a /> In preparing these  financial statements, the directors are required to:</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:  11.6pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">·</span></span><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;  color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">   </span>select suitable  accounting policies and then apply them consistently;</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:  11.6pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">·</span></span><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;  color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">   </span>make judgements and  accounting estimates that are reasonable and prudent;</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:  11.6pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">·</span></span><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;  color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">   </span>state whether applicable  accounting standards have been followed; and</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:11.6pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:  -11.6pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:11.6pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;  text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">·</span></span><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;  color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">   </span>prepare the financial  statements on the going concern basis unless it is inappropriate to<a /> presume that the company will continue in business.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><a /><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">The directors are responsible for keeping  proper accounting records that disclose with<a /> reasonable  accuracy at any time the financial position of the company and enable them to  ensure that the financial statements comply with the Companies Act 2006. They  are also responsible for safeguarding the assets of the company and hence for  taking reasonable steps for the prevention and detection of fraud and other  irregularities.</span></p></ix:nonNumeric></div><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;line-height:.5pt;mso-line-height-rule: exactly;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; color:black"><span> </span></span></p></div><div><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB; mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br /></span></div><div class="Section10"><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><a /><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">We have audited the financial statements of Canary Wharf Contractors Limited for the year ended 31 December 2010 which comprise the Profit and Loss Account, Balance Sheet and the related Notes 1 to 19.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The financial reporting framework that has been applied in their preparation is applicable law and United Kingdom Accounting Standards (United Kingdom Generally Accepted Accounting Practice).</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">This report is made solely to the company's members, as a body, in accordance with Chapter 3<a /> of Part 16 of the Companies Act 2006.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Our audit work has been undertaken so that we might<a /> state to the company's members those matters we are required to state to them in an<a /> auditor's report and for no other purpose.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>To the fullest extent permitted by law, we do<a /> not accept or assume responsibility to anyone other than the company and the company's<a /> members, as a body, for our audit work, for this report, or for the opinions we have formed.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Respective responsibilities of directors and auditor</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">As explained more fully in the Directors' Responsibilities Statement, the directors are<a /> responsible for the preparation of the financial statements and for being satisfied that<a /> they give a true and fair view.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Our responsibility is to audit and express an opinion on<a /> the financial statements in accordance with applicable law and International Standards on<a /> Auditing (UK and Ireland).<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Those standards require us to comply with the Auditing Practices Board's (APB's) Ethical Standards for Auditors.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Scope of the audit of the financial statements</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">An audit involves obtaining evidence about the amounts and disclosures in the financial<a /> statements sufficient to give reasonable assurance that the financial statements are free<a /> from material misstatement, whether caused by fraud or error.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>This includes an assessment<a /> of: whether the accounting policies are appropriate to the company's circumstances and have<a /> been consistently applied and adequately disclosed; the reasonableness of significant<a /> accounting estimates made by the directors; and the overall presentation of the financial statements.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">Opinion on financial statements</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">In our opinion the financial statements:</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:11.6pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:  -11.6pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:11.6pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;  text-autospace:none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">·</span></span><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;  color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">   </span>give a true and fair view  of the state of the company's affairs as at 31 December 2010 and<a /> of its profit for the year then ended;</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:11.6pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">R J J LYONS</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span>DIRECTOR<ix:nonNumeric name="ns4:NameDirectorSigningAccounts" contextRef="CY_PERIOD_DIRECTOR3_R_J_J_LYONS" /></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;line-height:.5pt;mso-line-height-rule: exactly;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; color:black"><span> </span></span></p></div><div><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB; mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br /></span></div><div class="Section14"><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black">1.</span></span><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">     </span><span style="font-weight: bold">PRINCIPAL ACCOUNTING POLICIES</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>A summary of the principal accounting policies of the company, all of which have been<a /> applied consistently throughout the year and the preceding year, is set out below.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span><span style="font-weight: bold">Accounting convention</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span><span><ix:nonNumeric name="ns4:StatementOnBasisMeasurementPreparationAccounts" contextRef="CY_PERIOD">The  financial statements have been prepared under the historical cost convention  and in accordance with applicable United Kingdom accounting standards.</ix:nonNumeric></span> The financial statements have been prepared on the going concern basis as described in the Directors' Report.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>In accordance with the provisions of <span>FRS</span> 1 (Revised) the company is exempt from<a /> the requirements to prepare a cash flow statement, as it is a wholly-owned<a /> subsidiary of Canary Wharf Group plc, which has prepared a consolidated cash flow<a /> statement.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span><span style="font-weight: bold">Turnover</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span><span><ix:nonNumeric name="ns4:TurnoverPolicy" contextRef="CY_PERIOD">Turnover  which is stated net of VAT comprises amounts charged in respect of the<a xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml" /> provision of building services and revenues earned on long  term contracts</ix:nonNumeric></span>.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span><span style="font-weight: bold">Interest receivable and interest payable</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Interest receivable and payable are recognised in the period in which they fall<a /> due.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Interest earned on amounts received in advance of future construction work<a /> is deferred and included within creditors as a component of payments on account.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span><span style="font-weight: bold">Dividends</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Dividend distributions to the company's shareholders are recognised in the financial statements in the period in which the dividends are paid or approved by the company's shareholders.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span><span style="font-weight: bold">Work in progress</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Work in progress includes costs incurred under both construction and development contracts.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Work in progress on construction contracts is stated at the lower of cost and net<a /> realisable value.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Cost includes construction costs and development expenditure, including employee and related costs.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Development contracts are accounted for as long term contracts in accordance with<a /> SSAP9. Turnover on such contracts is calculated by reference to the estimated value<a /> of work performed to date as a proportion of the total anticipated cost of the<a /> project. Profit is recognised when the final outcome of the project can be assessed<a /> with reasonable certainty, by including in the profit and loss account turnover<a /> and related costs as contract activity progresses.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span><span style="font-weight: bold">Trade and other debtors</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Debtors are recognised initially at fair value.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>A provision for impairment is established where there is objective evidence that the company will not be able to collect all amounts due according to the original terms of the debtor concerned.</span></p></div><div><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB; mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br /></span></div><div class="Section15"><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span><span style="font-weight: bold">Trade and other creditors</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Trade and other creditors are stated at cost.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span><span style="font-weight: bold">Taxation</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Current tax is provided at amounts expected to be paid or recovered using the tax rates and laws that have been enacted or substantively enacted at the balance sheet date. The company is part of a UK group for group relief purposes and accordingly may take advantage of the group relief provisions whereby current taxable profits can be offset by current tax losses arising in other companies in that group.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The group's policy is that no payment will be made for tax losses surrendered under the group relief provisions.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Deferred tax assets and liabilities arise from timing differences between the recognition of gains and losses in the financial statements and their recognition in the corporation tax return.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Under <span>FRS</span> 19 deferred tax is recognised in respect of all timing differences that have originated but not reversed at the balance sheet date where transactions or events that result in an obligation to pay more tax in the future or a right to pay less tax in the future have occurred at the balance sheet date.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>A net deferred tax asset is regarded as recoverable and therefore recognised only when, on the basis of all available evidence, it can be regarded as more likely than not that there will be suitable taxable profits from which the future reversal of the underlying timing differences can be deducted.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Deferred tax is not recognised when fixed assets are revalued unless by the balance sheet date there is a binding agreement to sell the revalued assets and the gain or loss expected to arise on sale has been recognised in the financial statements.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Deferred tax is measured on a discounted basis to reflect the time value of money over the period between the balance sheet date and the dates on which it is estimated that the timing differences will reverse, or where the timing differences are not expected to reverse, a period not exceeding 50 years.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Discount rates of 0.4% to 2.5% have been adopted reflecting the post-tax yield to maturity that can be obtained on government bonds with similar maturity dates and currencies to those of the deferred tax assets or liabilities.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span><span style="font-weight: bold">Pensions</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>The company operates a defined contribution pension scheme. Pension contributions in respect of this scheme are accrued as they fall due.</span></p></div><div><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB; mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br /></span></div><div class="Section16"><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span><span style="font-weight: bold">Accounting for share options</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>The economic cost to the company of share option schemes is charged to the same expense category as the employment cost of the relevant employee, spread on a straight line basis over the relevant performance criteria period.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>The economic cost represents either the acquisition cost of the shares or the market value of the shares at the date the options are granted, less any amount recoverable from the employee.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Where relevant, provision is made for employers' National Insurance contributions based on the market value of the share options at the balance sheet date and spread on a straight line basis over the period of the relevant performance criteria.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><a /><span style="font-weight: bold"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; color:black">2.</span></span><a /><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1">     </span><span style="font-weight: bold">TURNOVER</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>An analysis of turnover is given below:</span></p><table class="MsoNormalTable" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="margin-left:23.2pt;border-collapse:collapse;mso-table-layout-alt:fixed; color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">     </span><span style="font-weight: bold">OPERATING PROFIT</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none"><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span> </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>Operating profit is stated after charging:</span></p><table class="MsoNormalTable" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="margin-left:23.2pt;border-collapse:collapse;mso-table-layout-alt:fixed;  mso-padding-alt:0in 1.25pt 0in 1.25pt"><tr style="mso-yfti-irow:0;mso-yfti-firstrow:yes"><td valign="top" style="width:268.55pt;padding:0in 1.25pt 0in 1.25pt;width:358;"><a /><a /><p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none"><a /><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1">        </span>As part of the Canary Wharf Group pension arrangements, the company participates in a<a /> defined contribution pension scheme.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The assets of the scheme are held separately from<a /> those of the company in an independently administered fund.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The pension cost charge,<a /> which amounted to £<span><ix:nonFraction name="ns4:PensionsCostsDefinedContributionSchemes" contextRef="CY_PERIOD" unitRef="GBP" decimals="0" scale="0" format="ixt:numcommadot">1,455,668</ix:nonFraction></span> for the year (2009: £<span><ix:nonFraction name="ns4:PensionsCostsDefinedContributionSchemes" contextRef="PY_PERIOD" unitRef="GBP" decimals="0" scale="0" format="ixt:numcommadot">1,869,208</ix:nonFraction></span>), represents contributions<a /> payable by the company to the scheme.</span></p></div><div><span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;
